
namespace = spleasure

# BE WARNED, there's some creepy stuff here. And the cold and crude language of coding will make it look even more nasty.
# spleasure.1 umbrella event

# spleasure.2-56 temptation events
# spleasure.57-67 mutation events

# spleasure 68-91 don't remember
# spleasure.92-15905 Quirking Events

# spleasure.160-X Polymorph Events
# NEVER USE A SUSPICIOUS EVENT_IMAGE FOR THE TEMPTATION EVENT. THE PLAYER MUST NOT KNOW WHAT'S HE'S GETTING INTO.

# THE CHARACTER IS PRIMED BY A TEMPTATION EVENT WHEN HE GAINS THE SPIRITUALLYTEMPTED_SLAANESH/PHYSICALLYTEMPTED_SLAANESH FLAG.
# Once he has the flag, another umbrella event is activated to determine what happens when a courtiers nag him (at that point, depending on the choice, the character becomes a full cultist, gains the proper flag and unlocks the targetted decision).

# MAIN FLAGS IN USE:
# elf_slaaneshi_cultist

# spirituallytempted_slaanesh
# physicallytempted_slaanesh

# Umbrella event (called on_action) for spontaneous conversion
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.1
	hide_window = yes
	only_playable = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 40		# elves

	trigger = {
		trait = creature_elf
		nor = {
			religion = cult_of_pleasure
			religion = atharti
			society_member_of = cult_of_pleasure
			has_character_flag = spirituallytempted_slaanesh
			has_character_flag = physicallytempted_slaanesh
			has_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_conversion
			trait = malekith
			trait = everqueen
		}
		OR = {
			religion = cadai
			religion = cytharai
		}
		OR = {
			trait = scholar
			trait = poet
			trait = mystic
			trait = brilliant
			trait = quick
			trait = genius
			trait = hedonist
			trait = gluttonous
			trait = drunkard
			trait = cruel
			trait = impaler
			trait = temperate
			trait = chaste
			trait = celibate
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.75
			ai = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			ai = no
			has_focus = focus_seduction
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.50
			higher_tier_than = DUKE
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = stressed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = depressed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = fat
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = undernourished
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = addict
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = seducer
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = seductress
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = theologian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			trait = isolationist_elf
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			k_avelorn = {
				holder_scope = {
					trait = everqueen
					society_member_of = cult_of_pleasure
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			k_avelorn = {
				holder_scope = {
					trait = everqueen
					religion = cult_of_pleasure
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			religion = cytharai
			religion_authority = 0.50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			religion = cytharai
			religion_authority = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			religion = cadai
			religion_authority = 0.25
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			religion = cadai
			religion_authority = 0.50
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.1 for [Root.GetBestName]"
		random_list = {
			# Spiritual call
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_character_flag = temptation_won_poet
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						trait = poet
					}
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.2
				}
			}
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_character_flag = temptation_won_scholar
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						trait = scholar
					}
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.15
				}
			}
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_character_flag = temptation_won_mystic
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						trait = mystic
					}
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.22
				}
			}
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_character_flag = temptation_won_genius
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					nor = {
						trait = bright
						trait = smart
						trait = quick
						trait = brilliant
						trait = genius
					}
				}
				long_character_event = {
					id = spleasure.27
				}
			}
			# Physical call
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_character_flag = temptation_won_gluttonous
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					nor = {
						trait = hedonist
						trait = gluttonous
						trait = temperate
					}
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.32
				}
			}
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_character_flag = temptation_won_drunkard
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					nor = {
						trait = hedonist
						trait = drunkard
						trait = temperate
					}
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.39
				}
			}
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_character_flag = temptation_won_lustful
				}

# Poet has lost inspiration
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.2
	picture = GFX_evt_library
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCA_spleasure2
		trigger = {
			religion_group = cadai_group
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCB_spleasure2
		trigger = {
			religion_group = cytharai_group
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.2 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure2 # Use stuff
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.3
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure2 # Cut yourself
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCspleasure2 # No thanks
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_poet
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98
		}
	}
}

# Poet - A
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.3
	picture = GFX_evt_library
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCA_spleasure3
		trigger = {
			religion_group = cadai_group
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCB_spleasure3
		trigger = {
			religion_group = cytharai_group
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.3 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure3
		set_character_flag = spirituallytempted_slaanesh
		add_trait = addict
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.5
					}
				}
				30 = {
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.6
					}
				}
				25 = {
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.7
					}
				}
				5 = {
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.8
					}
				}	 # Tripping events
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = EVTOPTAspleasure4
		set_character_flag = spirituallytempted_slaanesh
		add_trait = wounded
		change_learning = 1
		long_character_event = {
			id = spleasure.12 days = 20 random = 60
		}
	}
}

# Tripping event 1
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.5
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_demons
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure5
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.5 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure5
		change_learning = 1
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = paranoid
				}
			}
			add_trait = paranoid
		}
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.9 days = 45 random = 50
		}
	}
}

# Tripping event 4
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.8
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_demons
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure8
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.8 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure8
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = brilliant
			}
			remove_trait = brilliant
			add_trait = genius
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = quick
			}
			remove_trait = quick
			add_trait = brilliant
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = smart
			}
			remove_trait = smart
			add_trait = quick
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = bright
			}
			remove_trait = bright
			add_trait = smart
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				nor = {
					trait = bright
					trait = smart
					trait = quick
					trait = brilliant
					trait = genius
				}
			}
			add_trait = bright
		}
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.9 days = 45 random = 50
		}
	}
}

# Servant making problems
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.9
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cult_1
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure9
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.9 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure9	# Have him join you
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.10
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure9	# Kill him of overdose
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.11
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCspleasure9	# Stop
		clr_character_flag = spirituallytempted_slaanesh
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_poet
		random_list = {
			80 = {
			}
			20 = {
				remove_trait = addict
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
	}
}

# Scholar annoyed by library student
long_character_event = {
	id = spleasure.18
	picture = GFX_evt_book_carolingian_script
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCA_spleasure18
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCB_spleasure18
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.18 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure18 # Have him lost
		trigger = {
			trait = deceitful
		}
		tooltip_info = deceitful
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.19
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure18 # Give him what he wants
		trigger = {
			trait = lustful
		}
		tooltip_info = lustful
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.20
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCspleasure18 # Have him fall from the stairs
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.21
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDspleasure18 # No thanks
		clr_character_flag = spirituallytempted_slaanesh
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_scholar
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
		}
	}
}

# Student gets it
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.20
	picture = GFX_evt_cult_of_pleasure

# Gluttonous/Temperate event
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.32
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCA_spleasure32
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
			trait = gluttonous
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCB_spleasure32
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
			trait = gluttonous
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCC_spleasure32
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
			trait = temperate
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCD_spleasure32
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
			trait = temperate
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCE_spleasure32
		trigger = {
			nor = {
				trait = temperate
				trait = gluttonous
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.32 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure32 # They're wrong, I'm fine!
		trigger = {
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.33
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure32 # Maybe a little moderation?
		trigger = {
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = {
			}
			40 = {
				remove_trait = gluttonous
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_gluttonous
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCspleasure32 # I little indulgement won't hurt...
		trigger = {
			trait = temperate
		}
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.34
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDspleasure32 # No thanks
		trigger = {
			trait = temperate
		}
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_gluttonous
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTEspleasure32 # What's wrong with having some fun?
		trigger = {
			nor = {
				trait = temperate
				trait = gluttonous
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = {
			}
			20 = {
				add_trait = drunkard
			}
			20 = {
				add_trait = gluttonous
			}
		}
		long_character_event = {
			id = spleasure.35
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTFspleasure32 # Let's keep it classy
		trigger = {
			nor = {
				trait = temperate
				trait = gluttonous
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_gluttonous
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_feast
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure45
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.45 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure45
		add_trait = addict
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.56
		}			# You unlocked the twist targetted decision
	}
}

# Lustful/chaste event
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.46
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCA_spleasure46
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
			religion_group = cadai_group
			trait = lustful
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCB_spleasure46
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
			religion_group = cadai_group
			trait = lustful
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCC_spleasure46
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
			religion_group = cytharai_group
			trait = lustful
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCD_spleasure46
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
			religion_group = cytharai_group
			trait = lustful
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCE_spleasure46
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
			religion_group = cadai_group
			NOT = {
				trait = lustful
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCF_spleasure46
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
			religion_group = cadai_group
			NOT = {
				trait = lustful
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCG_spleasure46
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
			religion_group = cytharai_group
			NOT = {
				trait = lustful
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCH_spleasure46
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
			religion_group = cytharai_group
			NOT = {
				trait = lustful
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.46 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure46 # Huuh! Kinky!
		trigger = {
			trait = lustful
		}
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.47
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure46 # That's not really my sort of things...
		trigger = {
			trait = lustful
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = {
			}
			40 = {
				remove_trait = lustful
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_lustful
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTEspleasure46 # Maybe.. just this once?
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				trait = lustful
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = celibate
			}
			remove_trait = celibate
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = {
			}
			40 = {
				add_trait = lustful
			}
		}
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.49
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTFspleasure46 # How dare you!
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				trait = lustful
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_lustful
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_evt_cult_of_pleasure

		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}

		text = EVTDESCB_spleasure47
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	}

		set_character_flag = physicallytempted_slaanesh
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.48
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure47	# That's too much, stop!
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_lustful
	}
}

# Cruel/Kind event, clumsy servant
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.51
	picture = GFX_evt_falconing
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCA_spleasure51
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = impaler
				trait = cruel
			}
			religion_group = cytharai_group
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCB_spleasure51
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = impaler
				trait = cruel
			}
			religion_group = cadai_group
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCC_spleasure51
		trigger = {
			trait = kind
			religion_group = cytharai_group
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCD_spleasure51
		trigger = {
			trait = kind
			religion_group = cadai_group
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.51 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure51 # You miserable wretch!
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = impaler
				trait = cruel
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			70 = {
			}
			30 = {
				add_trait = wroth
			}
		}
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.52
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure51 # You know what? He's beneath me.
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = impaler
				trait = cruel
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = {
			}
			40 = {
				remove_trait = cruel
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_cruel
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTEspleasure51 # That's it! Now you're getting it!
		trigger = {
			trait = kind
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = {
			}
			40 = {
				remove_trait = kind
			}
		}
		character_event = {
			id = spleasure.54
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTFspleasure51 # Don't worry, I can manage...
		trigger = {
			trait = kind
		}
		set_character_flag = temptation_won_cruel
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98
		}
	}
}

# MUTATION EVENTS
# The character did some nasty thing, he receives a gift from the Dark Prince

# Umbrella event
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.57
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.57 for [Root.GetBestName]"
		random_list = {
			# Tongue
			# Horns
			# Beauty
			# Ugliness
			# Madness
			# Gender swap
			35 = {
 				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = creature_elf
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.5705
				}
			}
			30 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = creature_elf
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.58
				}
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = creature_elf
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.59
				}
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = creature_elf
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.60
				}
			}
			5 = {
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.61
				}
			}
			5 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					nor = {
						trait = creature_elf
						trait = creature_human
						trait = creature_halfling
						trait = creature_dwarf
						trait = creature_chaos_dwarf
						trait = creature_amazon
						trait = creature_beastman
					}
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.171
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Mutation - Tongue
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.5705
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure57
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.5705 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure57	# hide it with magic
		trigger = {
			wh_is_mage_trigger = yes
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
 				modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					has_character_flag = hidden_mutation
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.62 days = 15 random = 23
				}
			}	# Success
			50 = {
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.63 days = 15 random = 24
				}
			}	# Failure
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure57	# hide it with intrigue
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		random_list = {
			40 = {
 				modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					NOT = {
						intrigue = 10
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					intrigue = 10
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					intrigue = 15
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					intrigue = 20
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					has_character_flag = hidden_mutation
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.62 days = 15 random = 23
				}
			}	# Success
			60 = {
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.63 days = 15 random = 24
				}
			}	# Failure
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCspleasure57
		add_trait = mut_tongue
		change_variable = {
			which = "mutation_counter"
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = {
				id = mutation.1001
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					religion = atharti
					religion = cult_of_pleasure
					religion = slaanesh
				}
			}
			# character_event = { id = spleasure.65 } 	# cultist exposed only when hidden
			increase_visibility_effect = yes # increase visibility
		}
	}
}

# Mutation - Horns

	id = spleasure.58
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure58
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.58 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure58	# hide it with magic
		trigger = {
			wh_is_mage_trigger = yes
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
 				modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					has_character_flag = hidden_mutation
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.62 days = 15 random = 23
				}
			}	# Success
			50 = {
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.64 days = 15 random = 24
				}
			}	# Failure
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure58	# hide it with intrigue
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		random_list = {
			40 = {
 				modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					NOT = {
						intrigue = 10
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.25
					intrigue = 10
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					intrigue = 15
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					intrigue = 20
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					has_character_flag = hidden_mutation
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.62 days = 15 random = 23
				}
			}	# Success
			60 = {
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.64 days = 15 random = 24
				}
			}	# Failure
		}

	option = {

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					religion = atharti
					religion = cult_of_pleasure
					religion = slaanesh
				}
			}
			character_event = {
				id = spleasure.65
			} 	# cultist exposed only when hidden
			increase_visibility_effect = yes # increase visibility
		}
	}
}

# Mutation - Beauty
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.59
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cult_1
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure59
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.59 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure59
		change_variable = {
			which = "mutation_counter"
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = {
				id = mutation.1001
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = pretty
			}
			remove_trait = pretty
			add_trait = beautiful
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = fair
			}
			remove_trait = fair
			add_trait = pretty
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = beautiful
					trait = pretty
					trait = fair
				}
				OR = {
					trait = plain
					trait = ugly
					trait = unsightly
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_trait = plain
				remove_trait = ugly
				remove_trait = unsightly
			}
			add_trait = fair
		}
	}
}

# Mutation - Ugliness
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.60
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cult_2
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure60
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.60 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure60
		change_variable = {
			which = "mutation_counter"
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = {
				id = mutation.1001
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = ugly
			}
			remove_trait = ugly
			add_trait = unsightly
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = plain
			}
			remove_trait = plain
			add_trait = ugly
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = ugly
					trait = plain
					trait = unsightly
				}
				OR = {
					trait = pretty
					trait = beautiful
					trait = fair
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_trait = pretty
				remove_trait = fair
				remove_trait = beautiful
			}
			add_trait = plain
		}
	}
}

# Mutation - Insanity
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.61
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cultist
	desc = EVTDESCA_spleasure61
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.61 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure61
		hidden_tooltip = {
			change_variable = {
				which = "lunatic_counter"
				value = 1
			}
			character_event = {
				id = mutation.1005
			}
		} # lunacy
	}

character_event = {
	id = spleasure.76
	desc = "EVTDESC1016"
	picture = "GFX_evt_lunatic"
	hide_from = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.76 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1016"
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_trait = paranoid 		# cheating cultist
			FROM = {
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.77
				}
			}
	# notify and choose what to do
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cynical
				NOT = {
					trait = charitable
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 45
				add_trait = paranoid
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38275 # Notify Paranoid
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = charitable
				NOT = {
					trait = cynical
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 10
				add_trait = paranoid
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38275 # Notify Paranoid
					}
				}
			}
		}

					trait = charitable

			}

				add_trait = paranoid
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {

						id = 38275 # Notify Paranoid
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# notify and choose what to do

				}
			}

				add_trait = trusting

		}

				}
			}
	# notify and choose what to do
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB65040
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.83
				}
			}
	# notify and choose what to do
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = gluttonous
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_dlc = "Reapers"
					}
				}
				add_trait = ill
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Reapers"
				}
				add_food_poisoning_symptom_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = gluttonous
				}
			}
			add_trait = gluttonous
		}
	}
}

				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 45
				add_trait = lustful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38272 # Notify Lustful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = slothful
				NOT = {
					trait = honest
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 10
				add_trait = lustful
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38272 # Notify Lustful
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {

				nor = {
					trait = honest
					trait = slothful
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 22
				add_trait = lustful
				hidden_tooltip = {

					}

				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38272 # Notify Lustful
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB1000"
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {

					id = spleasure.89
				}
			}
	# notify and choose what to do
		}
		if = {

				trait = arbitrary
				NOT = {
					trait = proud
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 45
				add_trait = chaste
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = {
						id = 38274 # Notify Chaste
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {

# Hiding disfigurement spell
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.90
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCAspleasure90
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = mut_spines
				trait = mut_horns
				trait = mut_scales
				trait = mut_thirdeye
				trait = mut_tongue
				trait = mut_crests
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCBspleasure90
		trigger = {
			nor = {
				trait = mut_spines
				trait = mut_horns
				trait = mut_scales
				trait = mut_thirdeye
				trait = mut_tongue
				trait = mut_crests
			}
			OR = {
				trait = disfigured
				trait = scarred
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCCspleasure90
		trigger = {
			nor = {
				trait = mut_spines
				trait = mut_horns
				trait = mut_scales
				trait = mut_thirdeye
				trait = mut_tongue
				trait = mut_crests
				trait = disfigured
				trait = scarred
			}
			trait = fat
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCDspleasure90
		trigger = {
			nor = {
				trait = mut_spines
				trait = mut_horns
				trait = mut_scales
				trait = mut_thirdeye
				trait = mut_tongue
				trait = mut_crests
				trait = disfigured
				trait = scarred
			}
			trait = undernourished
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_mage_lore_slaanesh
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.90 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure90
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = undernourished
				nor = {
					trait = disfigured
					trait = scarred
					trait = mut_spines
					trait = mut_horns
					trait = mut_scales
					trait = mut_thirdeye
					trait = mut_tongue
					trait = mut_crests
					has_character_modifier = hidden_disfigurement
				}
			}
			remove_trait = undernourished
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = hidden_undernourished
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = fat
				nor = {
					trait = disfigured
					trait = scarred
					trait = mut_spines
					trait = mut_horns
					trait = mut_scales
					trait = mut_thirdeye
					trait = mut_tongue
					trait = mut_crests
					has_character_modifier = hidden_disfigurement
					has_character_modifier = hidden_undernourished
				}
			}
			remove_trait = fat
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = hidden_fat
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = disfigured
					trait = scarred
				}
				nor = {
					trait = mut_spines
					trait = mut_horns
					trait = mut_scales
					trait = mut_thirdeye
					trait = mut_tongue
					trait = mut_crests
					has_character_modifier = hidden_fat
					has_character_modifier = hidden_disfigurement
					has_character_modifier = hidden_undernourished
				}
			}
			remove_trait = disfigured
			remove_trait = scarred
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = hidden_disfigurement
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = mut_spines
				nor = {
					has_character_modifier = hidden_fat
					has_character_modifier = hidden_undernourished
				}
			}
			remove_trait = mut_spines
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = hidden_spines
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = mut_horns
				nor = {
					has_character_modifier = hidden_fat
					has_character_modifier = hidden_undernourished
					has_character_modifier = hidden_spines
				}
			}
			remove_trait = mut_horns
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = hidden_horns
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = mut_scales
				nor = {
					has_character_modifier = hidden_fat
					has_character_modifier = hidden_undernourished
					has_character_modifier = hidden_spines
					has_character_modifier = hidden_horns
				}
			}
			remove_trait = mut_scales
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = hidden_scales
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = mut_thirdeye
				nor = {
					has_character_modifier = hidden_fat
					has_character_modifier = hidden_undernourished
					has_character_modifier = hidden_spines
					has_character_modifier = hidden_horns
					has_character_modifier = hidden_scales
				}
			}
			remove_trait = mut_thirdeye
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = hidden_thirdeye
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = mut_tongue
				nor = {
					has_character_modifier = hidden_fat
					has_character_modifier = hidden_undernourished
					has_character_modifier = hidden_spines
					has_character_modifier = hidden_horns
					has_character_modifier = hidden_scales
					has_character_modifier = hidden_thirdeye
				}
			}
			remove_trait = mut_tongue
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = hidden_tongue
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = mut_crests
				nor = {
					has_character_modifier = hidden_fat
					has_character_modifier = hidden_undernourished
					has_character_modifier = hidden_spines
					has_character_modifier = hidden_horns
					has_character_modifier = hidden_scales
					has_character_modifier = hidden_thirdeye
					has_character_modifier = hidden_tongue
				}
			}
			remove_trait = mut_crests
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = hidden_crests
				duration = 300
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				60 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						trait = brilliant
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						trait = genius
					}
				}
				40 = {
 					# Backfire
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = "doom_counter"
								value = 15
							}
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						check_variable = {
							which = "doom_counter"
							value = 60
						}
					}
					character_event = {

# Overview of the target
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.94
	desc = EVTDESCspleasure94
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cultist
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.94 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure94 # Don't like how he/she looks
		set_character_flag = s_changing_looks
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = spleasure.95
				days = 1
			}
			character_event = {
				id = spleasure.96
			}
		} # set integrity
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					trait = disfigured
					OR = {
						trait = fat
						trait = undernourished
					}
					OR = {
						trait = mut_horns
						trait = mut_scales
						trait = mut_crests
						trait = mut_tongue
						trait = mut_thirdeye
						trait = mut_spines
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = dim
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25

			}

						trait = beautiful
						trait = unsightly
						trait = fat
						trait = undernourished
						trait = disfigured
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5

					character = FROM
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75

					character = FROM
				}

					AND = {

							NOT = {

							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							is_female = yes
						}
						FROM = {
							is_female = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				OR = {
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								age = 50
							}
						}
						FROM = {
							OR = {
								trait = creature_human
								trait = creature_amazon
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								age = 1200
							}
						}
						FROM = {
							trait = creature_elf
						}
					}
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								age = 200
							}
						}
						FROM = {
							OR = {
								trait = creature_dwarf
								trait = creature_chaos_dwarf
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure94 # Don't like how he/she acts
		set_character_flag = s_changing_behavior
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = spleasure.95 days = 1
			}
			character_event = {

# Set integrity variable
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.96
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.96 for [Root.GetBestName]"
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = creature_human
					trait = creature_amazon
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = creature_elf
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = creature_dwarf
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = creature_chaos_dwarf
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = everqueen
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 9
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = phoenix_king
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 7
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = avatar_kurnous
			}

# Tricked (behavior)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.98004
	desc = EVTDESCspleasure98004
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_cultist
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.98004 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure98004 # Tricked
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				change_intrigue = 1
				set_character_flag = fake_skill_s
			}
			50 = {
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = fake_skill_s
				} 	# Slaanesh rigs the game for your enjoyment
				random_list = {
					99 = {
						change_intrigue = -1
						clr_character_flag = fake_skill_s
					}
					1 = {
						clr_character_flag = fake_skill_s
					}
				}
			}
		}

# The target was flattered, decide the improvement
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.99
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCAspleasure99
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_character_flag = refused_flattery_start
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCBspleasure99
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = refused_flattery_start
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_tempt
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.99 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure99 # Too plain
		FROM = {
			clr_character_flag = refused_flattery_start
			character_event = {
				id = spleasure.100 days = 5 random = 25
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 34
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				FROM = {
					trait = disfigured
					OR = {
						trait = mut_horns
						trait = mut_scales
						trait = mut_crests
						trait = mut_tongue
						trait = mut_thirdeye
						trait = mut_spines
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = scarred
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = disfigured
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.5
				trait = burnt_by_asuryan
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = inbred
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = unsightly
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = beautiful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

				id = spleasure.110 days = 5 random = 25
			}
		}

				}

				factor = 1.5

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = fat
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCspleasure99 # Too fat
		FROM = {
			clr_character_flag = refused_flattery_start
			character_event = {
				id = spleasure.120 days = 5 random = 25
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33

				factor = 0.1
				FROM = {

				}
			}

# Too plain - the target tries to improve it (hidden event pinging cultist and deciding the fate of the target)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.106
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.106 for [Root.GetBestName]"
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				FROM = {
					add_trait = scarred
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.107 days = 1
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					trait = scarred
				}
			}
			30 = {
				FROM = {
					add_trait = disfigured
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.108 days = 1
					}
				}
			}
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					FROM = {
						trait = beautiful
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					FROM = {
						wh_is_mage_trigger = no
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.75
					FROM = {
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					FROM = {
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					FROM = {
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 3
					FROM = {
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.109 days = 1
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							trait = pretty
						}
						remove_trait = pretty
						add_trait = beautiful
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							trait = fair
						}
						remove_trait = fair
						add_trait = pretty
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							nor = {
								trait = beautiful
								trait = pretty
								trait = fair
								trait = plain
								trait = ugly
								trait = unsightly
							}
						}
						add_trait = fair
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							trait = plain
						}
						remove_trait = plain
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							trait = ugly
						}
						remove_trait = ugly
						add_trait = plain
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							trait = unsightly
						}
						remove_trait = unsightly
						add_trait = ugly
					}
				}
			}
		}
	 	remove_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_quirking
		}
		FROM = {
			set_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 0
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Too thin - the target tries to improve it (hidden event pinging cultist and deciding the fate of the target)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.116
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.116 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	 	remove_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_quirking
		}
		FROM = {
			set_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 0
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
				years = 1
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = fat
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.119 days = 20 random = 30
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					nor = {
						trait = fat
						trait = undernourished
					}
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.118 days = 20 random = 30
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = undernourished
				}
				remove_trait = undernourished
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.117 days = 20 random = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Too fat - the target tries to improve it (hidden event pinging cultist and deciding the fate of the target)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.126
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.126 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	 	remove_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_quirking
		}
		FROM = {
			set_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 0
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
				years = 1
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = undernourished
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.129 days = 20 random = 30
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					nor = {
						trait = fat
						trait = undernourished
					}
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.128 days = 20 random = 30
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = fat
				}
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.127 days = 20 random = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	hide_window = yes

		log = "work event id = spleasure.136 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	 	remove_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_quirking
		}
		FROM = {
			set_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 0
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
				years = 1
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				FROM = {
					remove_trait = celibate
					remove_trait = chaste
					add_trait = lustful
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.137 days = 1
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					trait = lustful
				}
			}
			30 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					FROM = {
						trait = cruel
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					remove_trait = kind
					add_trait = cruel
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.138 days = 1
					}
				}

			}
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					NOT = {
						trait = lustful
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.139 days = 1
					}
					add_trait = depressed
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

	}

	 	remove_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_quirking
		}
		FROM = {
			set_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 0
			}

				modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
				years = 1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

# Too Modest - the target tries to improve it (hidden event pinging cultist and deciding the fate of the target)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.146
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.146 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	 	remove_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_quirking
		}
		FROM = {
			set_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 0
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
				years = 1
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				FROM = {
					remove_trait = humble
					add_trait = proud
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.147 days = 1
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					trait = proud
				}
			}
			30 = {
				FROM = {
					remove_trait = content
					add_trait = ambitious
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.148 days = 1
					}
				}
			}
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					trait = proud
				}
				FROM = {
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.149 days = 1
					}
					remove_trait = kind
					add_trait = envious
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Too Serious - the target tries to improve it (hidden event pinging cultist and deciding the fate of the target)
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.156
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.156 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	 	remove_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_quirking
		}
		FROM = {
			set_variable = {
				which = "s_integrity"
				value = 0
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_recently_quirked
				years = 1
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				FROM = {
					remove_trait = temperate
					add_trait = drunkard
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.157 days = 1
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					trait = drunkard
				}
			}
			30 = {
				FROM = {
					remove_trait = temperate
					add_trait = hedonist
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.158 days = 1
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					trait = hedonist
				}
			}
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						trait = drunkard
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					character_event = {
						id = spleasure.159 days = 1
					}
					remove_trait = temperate
					add_trait = addict
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# The prisoner becomes monstrous

	desc = EVTDESCAspleasure161
	picture = GFX_evt_mage_lore_slaanesh
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.161 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure161
		set_graphical_culture = beastman_ungor
		add_trait = monstrous
		prisoner = no
		opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_polymorphed_me
			who = FROM
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						religion = cadai
					}
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_barbaric
						who = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					religion_group = cytharai_group
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_polymorphed_family_druchii
					who = FROM
				}
			}
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						religion_group = cytharai_group
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_polymorphed_family
					who = FROM
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = spleasure.16105
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

# A monstrous character makes a monstrous son
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.168
	hide_window = yes
	trigger = {
		graphical_culture = ungorgfx
		OR = {
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				trait = monstrous
			}
			father_even_if_dead = {
				trait = monstrous
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

		add_trait = monstrous
	}

			}
		}

			}
		}

					is_female = yes

# Agnatic/Enatic realms toss the new character out
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.16906
	only_rulers = yes
	desc = EVTDESCAspleasure16906
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCAspleasure16906

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_female = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCBspleasure16906

		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_bad_news
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				is_female = yes			 # the game still considers her a female
				primary_title = {
					has_law = enatic_succession
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_female = no			 # the game still considers him a female
				primary_title = {
					has_law = agnatic_succession
				}
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.16906 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure16906
		abdicate = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

	id = spleasure.16907
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCAspleasure16907

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_female = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCBspleasure16907

		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_mage_lore_slaanesh
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.16907 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure16907
		remove_trait = homosexual
		hidden_tooltip = {
			spouse = {
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.172 days = 150 random = 100
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

# The swap is complete (homosexual), notify spouse
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.172
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCAspleasure172
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_female = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCBspleasure172
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_mage_lore_slaanesh
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.172 for [Root.GetBestName]"
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAspleasure172
		trigger = {
			spouse = {
				wh_this_and_root_can_love_trigger = yes
			}
			OR = {
				trait = homosexual
				ai = no
			}
		} # A wish come true
		hidden_tooltip = {
			spouse = {
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.17205
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBspleasure172
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				trait = homosexual
			}
		} # This marriage is over
		hidden_tooltip = {
			spouse = {
				character_event = {
					id = spleasure.17206
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCspleasure172
		trigger = {
			ai = no
		} # I don't care
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

# Gender-swapped woman knocks up by spouse
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.175
	min_age = 15
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_women = yes
	hide_window = yes
	trigger = {
		trait = transgender
		nor = {
			trait = creature_orc
			trait = creature_goblin
			trait = creature_snotling
			trait = creature_nehekharan
		}
		is_vampire_trigger = no
		nor = {
			trait = celibate
			trait = infertile
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				age = 45
			}
			AND = {
				nor = {
					trait = creature_human
					trait = creature_halfling
				}
			}
		}
		is_pregnant = no
		spouse = {
			is_female = yes
			nor = {
				trait = eunuch
				trait = creature_orc
				trait = creature_goblin
				trait = creature_snotling
				trait = creature_nehekharan
			}
			is_vampire_trigger = no
			# To avoid halfbreeds
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = {
						trait = creature_human
					}
					trait = creature_human
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = {
						trait = creature_amazon
					}
					trait = creature_amazon
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = {
						trait = creature_elf
					}
					trait = creature_elf
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = {
						trait = creature_halfling
					}
					trait = creature_halfling
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = {
						trait = creature_dwarf
					}
					trait = creature_dwarf
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = {
						trait = creature_chaos_dwarf
					}
					trait = creature_chaos_dwarf
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = {
						trait = creature_skaven
					}
					trait = creature_skaven
				}
			}
			is_alive = yes
			nor = {
				trait = incapable
				has_character_modifier = stage_progressed
			} # so that the consorts will cycle
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 15
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.75
			trait = creature_elf
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 45
			in_command = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.45
			trait = retired_with_harem
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.15
			has_character_modifier = horny_harem_mod
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = lustful

# Ping spouse
character_event = {
	id = spleasure.176
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "work event id = spleasure.176 for [Root.GetBestName]"
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = wh_concubine.9
			}
		}
	}
}
